# 7) README
readme = textwrap.dedent(f"""
# PureTask n8n Workflows

This folder contains importable n8n workflows for the core PureTask automations.

## Files
1. `01_recurring_plan_generator.json` – Nightly plan scan → generate next 14 days of occurrences.
2. `02_job_creation_from_occurrences.json` – 5 days ahead, converts occurrences to jobs + escrow holds.
3. `03_weekly_payout_processor.json` – Friday 18:00 UTC, batches earnings and executes Stripe Connect payouts.
4. `04_auto_refill.json` – Hourly low-balance sweep, creates PaymentIntent and credits wallet.
5. `05_subscription_renewal_webhook.json` – Webhook for Stripe `invoice.paid` → credits wallet.
6. `06_reliability_tier_update.json` – Webhook on job approval → writes reliability events and recalculates tier.

## How to import
- In n8n, click **Workflows ▸ Import from File**. Import each JSON.
- Edit each HTTP Request node to point to your API base (currently `{API_BASE}`) and add auth headers.
- Toggle **Active** on the workflows you want live.
- Change Cron schedules if needed.

## Environment
Set these as n8n credentials or environment variables:
- API auth (JWT/API key)
- STRIPE_SECRET_KEY, STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET (if using n8n as webhook handler)
- DB credentials if using direct DB nodes instead of HTTP

## Notes
- Bodies sent to your API are simple JSON stubs. Map them to your Base44 endpoints that implement the logic we defined (escrow, final charge, refunds, earnings, payouts, subscriptions, auto-refill, reliability).
- All times are UTC. Adjust cron rules to PT if your n8n server runs local time.
- Test on staging first, then enable in production.
""").strip()

with open(os.path.join(base, "README_n8n.md"), "w") as f:
    f.write(readme)

# Create ZIP
zip_path = "/mnt/data/PureTask_n8n_Workflows.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    for fname in os.listdir(base):
        fpath = os.path.join(base, fname)
        if os.path.isfile(fpath):
            z.write(fpath, arcname=fname)

# Return directory listing and zip path
sorted(os.listdir(base)), zip_path

import os, json, textwrap, zipfile, datetime

base = "/mnt/data/n8n_puretask"
os.makedirs(base, exist_ok=True)

def write_json(path, data):
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

now_iso = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"
API_BASE = "https://api.puretask.internal"  # placeholder; replace in n8n

provide me more business focused and money focused quesitons

Excellent question — here’s a comprehensive, high-value list of business- and money-focused questions you should ask your PureTask AI (or yourself as the founder) to keep the platform profitable, scalable, and strategically aligned.

Each question includes why it matters — so your AI co-founder can respond with clarity and give you financial insight, not just data.

💰 1. REVENUE & PRICING STRATEGY
These define how money moves through PureTask and how to maximize profit per transaction.

Questions to Ask:

“What is our profit margin per job after cleaner payouts and platform fees?”

“How can we increase average booking value without raising prices?”

“What happens to revenue if we shift payout frequency from weekly to biweekly?”

“Which cleaning type (basic / deep / move-out) generates the best ROI?”

“How can we design pricing tiers that encourage upsells (e.g., Bronze → Silver)?”

“Should we charge transaction fees, subscription plans, or both?”

“What’s the revenue potential of recurring clients vs. one-time clients?”

“How much should we hold in escrow to maintain liquidity and trust?”

“At what point does the credit float become an investable cash asset?”

“How can we bundle credits to encourage larger upfront purchases?”

Why ask:
→ Helps the AI model cash flow mechanics, find leaks, and build monetization strategies.

📊 2. FINANCIAL FORECASTING & SCALING
These guide long-term sustainability, investor readiness, and operational scaling.

Questions to Ask:

“What are our key financial KPIs (CAC, LTV, retention, churn)?”

“How many active recurring clients do we need to reach $10K/month in profit?”

“What are the top 3 financial levers that move PureTask toward profitability?”

“How should we forecast recurring revenue based on booking frequency?”

“What’s the breakeven point per city or region?”

“How should we model our cleaner acquisition cost vs. revenue per cleaner?”

“At what stage should we introduce corporate/commercial cleaning plans?”

“If we double recurring clients, what infrastructure costs increase?”

Why ask:
→ Lets AI run growth simulations and budget planning, giving you investor-ready models.

🧩 3. UNIT ECONOMICS
To ensure every transaction is profitable before scale.

Questions to Ask:

“What’s the cost per job (support, payment fees, overhead)?”

“What is our take rate (%) and how does it compare to competitors?”

“If 1 credit = $0.10, how do fees and payouts affect each side’s value?”

“How does our tier payout percentage affect net margin per booking?”

“How do cancellation rates or refunds impact gross margin?”

Why ask:
→ AI can simulate pricing elasticity, showing where you lose or gain per job.

⚙️ 4. CUSTOMER LIFETIME VALUE (LTV) OPTIMIZATION
How to turn one-time clients into repeat buyers.

Questions to Ask:

“How many bookings does the average client make before churning?”

“What retention tactics improve LTV the fastest?”

“How can we use credits or rewards to lock clients into recurring plans?”

“What messages convert first-time clients into subscribers?”

“What’s the optimal incentive for referrals that doesn’t erode margin?”

Why ask:
→ AI can help design automation triggers and loyalty incentives.

🧠 5. BUSINESS MODEL REFINEMENT
For strategic decisions & investor storytelling.

Questions to Ask:

“How should we describe our revenue model to investors?”

“Can we position PureTask as a marketplace + SaaS hybrid?”

“Should credits expire or roll over to create predictable cash flow?”

“How do we create tier-based rewards for cleaners that improve platform stickiness?”

“How much monthly float do we hold before payouts, and how do we use it?”

Why ask:
→ Enables AI to design models that balance growth with regulatory safety.

🧾 6. INVESTOR & FINANCIAL NARRATIVE
To attract funding and articulate the business value.

Questions to Ask:

“What metrics do investors care about most for marketplace startups?”

“How can we highlight our credit system as a growth lever, not a liability?”

“What financial story will show scalability and defensibility?”

“What’s the projected ARR with X users and Y average spend?”

“What is our exit or acquisition potential if we hit 10K active users?”

Why ask:
→ AI can build your investor deck, valuation models, and talking points.

🧮 7. COST CONTROL & PROFITABILITY
To make sure growth ≠ burn.

Questions to Ask:

“Where are we losing the most money operationally?”

“What percentage of revenue should go to cleaner payouts vs. marketing?”

“What’s the ideal marketing spend to customer LTV ratio?”

“What automations could cut admin costs by 30%?”

“How do we measure the ROI of each new feature or campaign?”

Why ask:
→ AI can recommend which automations, hires, or ads deliver the best ROI.

🧱 8. EXPANSION STRATEGY
How to scale locally, regionally, and nationally.

Questions to Ask:

“Which ZIP codes or cities have the highest demand per capita?”

“What’s the best order of expansion based on operational cost vs. return?”

“When should we onboard local managers or franchise partners?”

“How should pricing adjust across regions to maintain margins?”

“At what user count should we form a legal entity for each region?”

Why ask:
→ AI can cross-analyze population, cleaning demand, and cost data for market expansion maps.

how do u clear the cache

Here’s how to clear cache, depending on what device or browser you're using.

✅ Clear Cache on Google Chrome (Windows / Mac)
Open Chrome

Press:
Windows: Ctrl + Shift + Delete
Mac: Command + Shift + Delete

A popup will appear.

Select:

✅ Cookies and other site data

✅ Cached images and files

Time range → All time

Click Clear data

✅ Clear Cache on Safari (Mac)
Click Safari (top menu)

Go to Settings → Advanced

Check "Show Develop menu in menu bar"

In top menu, click Develop

Click Empty Caches

✅ Clear Cache on iPhone / iPad (Safari)
Go to Settings

Scroll to Safari

Tap Clear History and Website Data

✅ Clear Cache on Android (Chrome)
Open Chrome

Tap ⋮ (three dots) → History

Tap Clear browsing data

Select:

Cached images and files

Cookies/site data

Confirm Clear data

✅ Clear Cache on Windows PC (full system cache)
Press Windows Key + R

Type:

%temp%
Select everything → Delete

Optional deeper clean:

Press Windows Key + R

Type:

temp
Delete files

✅ Clear Cache on Mac (full system cache)
Open Finder

Go to menu Go → Go to Folder

Type:

~/Library/Caches
Delete contents (not the folder itself)

🤝 Want me to guide you live?
Tell me:
➡️ What device (Windows / Mac / iPhone / Android)
➡️ What browser (Chrome / Safari etc.)

Example reply:

“Mac + Chrome”
or
“iPhone Safari”

…and I'll give exact step-by-step visuals tailored to you.

Open Opera

Click the Opera logo / Menu icon (top-left corner)

Go to:

Settings (Mac: Opera → Preferences)

On the left sidebar, click:

Privacy & Security

Find:

Clear browsing data…

A pop-up will appear.

Select these options:

✅ Cached images and files

(Optional) ✅ Cookies and other site data

At the top, change Time range to:

➤ All time

Click Clear data

⚡ Shortcut method:
Press this on keyboard:

Windows: Ctrl + Shift + Delete

Mac: Command + Shift + Delete

It will instantly open the Clear Browsing Data window.

🔧 Extra step (recommended)
Clear Opera’s internal media cache:

In the address bar, type:

opera://net-internals/#dns
Click Clear host cache

🧨 Restart Browser
After clearing cache:

Fully close Opera

Reopen it

If you’re doing this because your app (Base44, PureTask UI, etc.) isn’t updating, you may also need to do a hard refresh:

Windows: Ctrl + F5

Mac: Command + Shift + R

If you want, I can walk you through clearing the profile cache, delete Service Worker files, or reset local storage depending on what issue you're having.

Just tell me:

“Opera won’t update my page”
or
“Base44 keeps showing old changes”

…and I’ll target the fix.
